Q. I have a strong image like a girl. I wonder if you feel the limitations or weaknesses of these images, or if you think they are unique to your group.
A. Beanie) The girly and fairy tale atmosphere is Oh My Girl's strength. It's also the color we can best express. Oh my girl through the queen
